<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" width="30" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="1376" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1942" class="extiw" title="commons:Category:1942">1942</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1942 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMXLII</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Thursday" title="Common year starting on Thursday">starting on Thursday</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1942nd year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 942nd year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd&#160;millennium</a>, the 42nd year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th&#160;century</a>, and the 3rd year of the <a href="/wiki/1940s" title="1940s">1940s</a> decade.</p>
<div class="toclimit-2">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Below, events of <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a> have the "WWII" prefix.</p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:World_War_II_in_Europe,_1942.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg/220px-World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg.png" width="220" height="207" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg/330px-World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg/440px-World_War_II_in_Europe%2C_1942.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="519" data-file-height="488" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:World_War_II_in_Europe,_1942.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of Europe at the height of German control in 1942, Britain remaining the only country in Western Europe held by Allied forces</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_1" title="January 1">January 1</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Declaration_by_United_Nations" title="Declaration by United Nations">Declaration by United Nations</a> is signed by China, the United Kingdom, the United States, the Soviet Union and 22 other nations, in which they agree "not to make any separate peace with the Axis powers".</li>
<li>United States and <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> troops fight the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Bataan" title="Battle of Bataan">Battle of Bataan</a> against Japanese forces.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_2" title="January 2">January 2</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>Japanese warplanes bomb <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>, Philippines.</li>
<li>Activation of the United States <a href="/wiki/Eighth_Air_Force" title="Eighth Air Force">Eighth Air Force</a> in <a href="/wiki/Savannah,_Georgia" title="Savannah, Georgia">Savannah, Georgia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_7" title="January 7">January 7</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Operation_Typhoon" class="mw-redirect" title="Operation Typhoon">Operation Typhoon</a>, the German attempt to take Moscow, ends in failure.</li>
<li>The siege of the <a href="/wiki/Bataan_Peninsula" class="mw-redirect" title="Bataan Peninsula">Bataan Peninsula</a> begins.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_11" title="January 11">January 11</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_Indies_campaign" title="Dutch East Indies campaign">Dutch East Indies campaign</a>: Japan declares war on the Netherlands and invades the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_Indies" title="Dutch East Indies">Dutch East Indies</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malayan_Campaign" title="Malayan Campaign">Malayan Campaign</a>: The Japanese capture <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, the capital of the <a href="/wiki/Federated_Malay_States" title="Federated Malay States">Federated Malay States</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_13" title="January 13">January 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sikorsky_R-4" title="Sikorsky R-4">Sikorsky R-4</a> first flies, in the United States; it will become the first mass-produced <a href="/wiki/Helicopter" title="Helicopter">helicopter</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Heinkel" title="Heinkel">Heinkel</a> test pilot Helmut Schenk becomes the first person to escape from a stricken aircraft with an <a href="/wiki/Ejection_seat" title="Ejection seat">ejection seat</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_16" title="January 16">January 16</a> – American film actress <a href="/wiki/Carole_Lombard" title="Carole Lombard">Carole Lombard</a> and her mother are among all 22 aboard <a href="/wiki/TWA_Flight_3" title="TWA Flight 3">TWA Flight 3</a> killed when the <a href="/wiki/Douglas_DC-3" title="Douglas DC-3">Douglas DC-3</a> plane crashes into <a href="/wiki/Potosi_Mountain_(Nevada)" title="Potosi Mountain (Nevada)">Potosi Mountain</a> near <a href="/wiki/Las_Vegas" title="Las Vegas">Las Vegas</a> while she is returning from a tour to promote the sale of war bonds.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_19" title="January 19">January 19</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>Japanese forces invade <a href="/wiki/Burma" class="mw-redirect" title="Burma">Burma</a>.</li>
<li>Establishment of Commands of the United States <a href="/wiki/Eighth_Air_Force" title="Eighth Air Force">Eighth Air Force</a>: VIII Bomber Command initially at <a href="/wiki/Langley_Field" class="mw-redirect" title="Langley Field">Langley Field</a> in Virginia and <a href="/wiki/VIII_Fighter_Command" title="VIII Fighter Command">VIII Fighter Command</a> at <a href="/wiki/Selfridge_Air_National_Guard_Base" title="Selfridge Air National Guard Base">Selfridge Field</a> in Michigan.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_20" title="January 20">January 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: <a href="/wiki/Nazism" title="Nazism">Nazis</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Wannsee_Conference" title="Wannsee Conference">Wannsee Conference</a> in Berlin decide that the "<a href="/wiki/Final_Solution" title="Final Solution">Final Solution</a> (<i>Endlösung</i>) to the Jewish problem" is relocation, and later extermination.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_21" title="January 21">January 21</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Erwin_Rommel" title="Erwin Rommel">Erwin Rommel</a> launches his new offensive in <a href="/wiki/Cyrenaica" title="Cyrenaica">Cyrenaica</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_23" title="January 23">January 23</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Rabaul_(1942)" title="Battle of Rabaul (1942)">Battle of Rabaul</a> begins.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> declares war on the United States and United Kingdom.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a> – WWII: The first American forces arrive in Europe, landing in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_31" title="January 31">January 31</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Malayan_Campaign" title="Malayan Campaign">Malayan Campaign</a>: The last organized Allied forces leave <a href="/wiki/British_Malaya" title="British Malaya">British Malaya</a>, ending the 54-day campaign, and the <a href="/wiki/Johor%E2%80%93Singapore_Causeway" title="Johor–Singapore Causeway">Johor–Singapore Causeway</a> is severed.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>February – <a href="/wiki/C._S._Lewis" title="C. S. Lewis">C. S. Lewis</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/The_Screwtape_Letters" title="The Screwtape Letters">The Screwtape Letters</a></i> first published in book format in England.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> – WWII: The Command staff of the <a href="/wiki/VIII_Bomber_Command" class="mw-redirect" title="VIII Bomber Command">Eighth Air Force</a> reaches England.</li>
<li>February 1 – <a href="/wiki/Mao_Zedong" title="Mao Zedong">Mao Zedong</a> makes a speech on "Reform in Learning, the Party and Literature." This starts <a href="/wiki/Yan%27an_Rectification_Movement" title="Yan'an Rectification Movement">Yan'an Rectification Movement</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_3" title="February 3">February 3</a> – WWII: Rommel suspends his offensive in Cyrenaica.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_7" title="February 7">February 7</a> – <a href="/wiki/United_States_Maritime_Commission" title="United States Maritime Commission">United States Maritime Commission</a> fleet operations transferred to the <a href="/wiki/War_Shipping_Administration" title="War Shipping Administration">War Shipping Administration</a> (lasting until <a href="/wiki/September_1" title="September 1">September 1</a>, <a href="/wiki/1946" title="1946">1946</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_8" title="February 8">February 8</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_%C3%93scar_Carmona" class="mw-redirect" title="António Óscar Carmona">António Óscar Carmona</a> is elected president of Portugal.</li>
<li>WWII: Top United States military leaders hold their first formal meeting to discuss American military strategy in the war.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Daylight_saving_time" title="Daylight saving time">Daylight saving time</a> goes into effect in the United States.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_9" title="February 9">February 9</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Ocean_liner" title="Ocean liner">ocean liner</a> <a href="/wiki/SS_Normandie" title="SS Normandie">SS&#160;<i>Normandie</i></a> catches fire while being converted into the troopship USS <i>Lafayette</i> (AP-53) for WWII at pier 88 in New York City: she capsizes early the following morning.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_11" title="February 11">February 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Operation_Cerberus" class="mw-redirect" title="Operation Cerberus">Operation Cerberus</a>: A flotilla of <a href="/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a> ships dash from <a href="/wiki/Brest,_France" title="Brest, France">Brest</a> through the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a> to northern ports; the British fail to sink any of them.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_15" title="February 15">February 15</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Singapore" title="Battle of Singapore">Singapore surrenders to Japanese</a> forces.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_18" title="February 18">February 18</a> – WWII: More than 200 American sailors die in <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Newfoundland and Labrador">Newfoundland</a> when the <a href="/wiki/USS_Truxtun_(DD-229)" title="USS Truxtun (DD-229)">USS&#160;<i>Truxtun</i></a> runs aground near Chambers Cove and the <a href="/wiki/USS_Pollux_(AKS-2)" title="USS Pollux (AKS-2)">USS&#160;<i>Pollux</i></a> runs aground at Lawn Point.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_19" title="February 19">February 19</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bombing_of_Darwin" title="Bombing of Darwin">Japanese warplanes bomb Darwin</a>, Australia.</li>
<li>A returning Japanese fighter plane crashes on <a href="/wiki/Melville_Island_(Australia)" title="Melville Island (Australia)">Melville Island (Australia)</a> and its pilot, <a href="/wiki/Hajime_Toyoshima" title="Hajime Toyoshima">Hajime Toyoshima</a>, becomes the first Japanese captured on Australian soil when <a href="/wiki/Indigenous_Australians" title="Indigenous Australians">indigenous resident</a> <a href="/wiki/Matthias_Ulungura" title="Matthias Ulungura">Matthias Ulungura</a> takes him prisoner.</li>
<li>United States President <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a> signs <a href="/wiki/Executive_Order_9066" title="Executive Order 9066">Executive Order 9066</a> allowing the United States military to define areas as exclusionary zones. These zones affect the <a href="/wiki/Internment_of_Japanese_Americans" title="Internment of Japanese Americans">Japanese</a> on the West Coast, and <a href="/wiki/Internment_of_German_Americans" title="Internment of German Americans">Germans</a> and <a href="/wiki/Internment_of_Italian_Americans" title="Internment of Italian Americans">Italians</a> primarily on the East Coast.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_19" title="February 19">February 19</a>–<a href="/wiki/February_23" title="February 23">23</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sittang_Bridge" title="Battle of Sittang Bridge">Battle of Sittang Bridge</a> – British forces retreat to the <a href="/wiki/Sittaung_River" title="Sittaung River">Sittaung River</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_20" title="February 20">February 20</a> – Lieutenant <a href="/wiki/Edward_O%27Hare" title="Edward O'Hare">Edward O'Hare</a> becomes America's first U.S. Navy WWII <a href="/wiki/Flying_ace" title="Flying ace">flying ace</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_22" title="February 22">February 22</a> – General <a href="/wiki/George_Marshall" title="George Marshall">George Marshall</a> transmits a direct order to <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">General MacArthur</a> in <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">President Roosevelt</a>'s name, ordering MacArthur himself to turn over command of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> to a subordinate and report to Australia to assume command of the large American force being built up there. The orders are worded to allow MacArthur to choose the exact moment of his <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur%27s_escape_from_the_Philippines" title="Douglas MacArthur's escape from the Philippines">departure</a>; for various reasons, he will not leave until March 12 (Eastern Date).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_23" title="February 23">February 23</a> – The Japanese submarine <a href="/wiki/Japanese_submarine_I-17" title="Japanese submarine I-17"><i>I-17</i></a> fires 17 high-explosive shells toward an oil <a href="/wiki/Refinery" title="Refinery">refinery</a> near <a href="/wiki/Santa_Barbara,_California" title="Santa Barbara, California">Santa Barbara, California</a>, causing little damage.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_24" title="February 24">February 24</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Struma_disaster" title="Struma disaster"><i>Struma</i> disaster</a>: <a href="/wiki/MV_Struma" title="MV Struma">MV&#160;<i>Struma</i></a>, carrying Jewish refugees from Axis-allied Romania to British-administered Palestine, is torpedoed and sunk by the Soviet submarine <a href="/wiki/Soviet_submarine_Shch-213" title="Soviet submarine Shch-213"><i>Shch-213</i></a>, killing about 791 men, women and children, with only one survivor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Propaganda" title="Propaganda">Propaganda</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Voice_of_America" title="Voice of America">Voice of America</a> begins broadcasting.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_25" title="February 25">February 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Los_Angeles" title="Battle of Los Angeles">Battle of Los Angeles</a>: Over 1,400 AA shells are fired at an unidentified, slow-moving object in the skies over Los Angeles. The appearance of the object triggers an immediate wartime blackout over most of <a href="/wiki/Southern_California" title="Southern California">Southern California</a>, with thousands of air raid wardens being deployed throughout the city. In total there are 6 deaths. Despite the several-hour barrage no planes are downed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_26" title="February 26">February 26</a>
<ul>
<li>The worst <a href="/wiki/Coal_dust" title="Coal dust">coal dust</a> explosion to date, in Honkeiko, China, claims 1,549 lives.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/14th_Academy_Awards" title="14th Academy Awards">14th Academy Awards</a> ceremony is held in Los Angeles; <i><a href="/wiki/How_Green_Was_My_Valley_(film)" title="How Green Was My Valley (film)">How Green Was My Valley</a></i> wins <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">Best Picture</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_27" title="February 27">February 27</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Java_Sea" title="Battle of the Java Sea">Battle of the Java Sea</a>: An allied (<a href="/wiki/ABDA" class="mw-redirect" title="ABDA">ABDA</a>) task force of 14 vessels under <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> command, trying to stem a Japanese invasion of the <a href="/wiki/Dutch_East_Indies" title="Dutch East Indies">Dutch East Indies</a>, is defeated by a 19 vessel Japanese task force in the <a href="/wiki/Java_Sea" title="Java Sea">Java Sea</a>; 2.300 sailors die, including the commander, admiral <a href="/wiki/Karel_Doorman" title="Karel Doorman">Karel Doorman</a>; Japanese attain naval hegemony in East-Asia</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>March – Construction begins on the <a href="/wiki/Badger_Army_Ammunition_Plant" title="Badger Army Ammunition Plant">Badger Army Ammunition Plant</a>, the largest in the United States during WWII.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_9" title="March 9">March 9</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Executive_order" class="mw-redirect" title="Executive order">Executive order</a> 9082 (February 28, 1942) comes into effect reorganizing the United States Army into three major commands: <a href="/wiki/Army_Ground_Forces" title="Army Ground Forces">Army Ground Forces</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Forces" title="United States Army Air Forces">Army Air Forces</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Services_of_Supply" class="mw-redirect" title="Services of Supply">Services of Supply</a>, later redesignated <a href="/wiki/Army_Service_Forces" title="Army Service Forces">Army Service Forces</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Henry_H._Arnold" title="Henry H. Arnold">Henry H. Arnold</a> as Commanding General of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Forces" title="United States Army Air Forces">United States Army Air Forces</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a> – WWII: U.S. General <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">Douglas MacArthur</a>, his family, and key members of his staff are evacuated by <a href="/wiki/PT_boat" title="PT boat">PT boat</a>, under cover of darkness, from <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Corregidor" title="Battle of Corregidor">Corregidor</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. Command of U.S. forces in the Philippines passes to <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_M._Wainwright_(general)" title="Jonathan M. Wainwright (general)">Major General Jonathan M. Wainwright</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_15" title="March 15">March 15</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCnam%C3%BCnde_Action" title="Dünamünde Action">Dünamünde Action</a> takes place. 1,900 central European Jews are shot dead north east of <a href="/wiki/Riga" title="Riga">Riga</a>, 1,840 are killed on the 26th.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_16" title="March 16">March 16</a> – WWII: New Zealand and Australia declare war on <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_17" title="March 17">March 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: <a href="/wiki/Operation_Reinhard" title="Operation Reinhard">Operation Reinhard</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi German</a> <a href="/wiki/Be%C5%82%C5%BCec_extermination_camp" title="Bełżec extermination camp">Bełżec extermination camp</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%9345)" class="mw-redirect" title="Occupation of Poland (1939–45)">occupied Poland</a> about 1&#160;km south of the railroad station at <a href="/wiki/Be%C5%82%C5%BCec_extermination_camp" title="Bełżec extermination camp">Bełżec</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Lublin" title="Lublin">Lublin</a> district of the <a href="/wiki/General_Government" title="General Government">General Government</a>. At least 434,508 people are killed here up to December 1942.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_18" title="March 18">March 18</a> – <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a>, President of the United States, signs <a href="/wiki/Executive_Order_9102" title="Executive Order 9102">Executive Order 9102</a>, creating the <a href="/wiki/War_Relocation_Authority" title="War Relocation Authority">War Relocation Authority</a> (WRA), which becomes responsible for the internment of Americans of Japanese and, to a lesser extent, German and Italian descent, many of them legal citizens.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_20" title="March 20">March 20</a> – WWII: After being forced to flee the Philippines, U.S. General <a href="/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">Douglas MacArthur</a> announces (in <a href="/wiki/Terowie,_South_Australia" title="Terowie, South Australia">Terowie, South Australia</a>), "I came through and I shall return."<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_22" title="March 22">March 22</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Sirte" title="Second Battle of Sirte">Second Battle of Sirte</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">Mediterranean Sea</a> – Escorting warships of a British convoy to <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a> ward off a much more powerful <i><a href="/wiki/Regia_Marina" title="Regia Marina">Regia Marina</a></i> (Italian Navy) squadron north of the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Sirte" title="Gulf of Sirte">Gulf of Sirte</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_23" title="March 23">March 23</a> – WWII: The Germans burn down the Ukrainian village of Yelino (<a href="/wiki/Koriukivka_Raion" title="Koriukivka Raion">Koriukivka Raion</a>), killing 296 civilians.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_24" title="March 24">March 24</a> – The evacuation of Polish nationals from the Soviet Union begins. It is conducted in two phases: until 5 April; and between 10 and 30 August 1942, by sea from Krasnovodsk to Pahlavi (Anzali), and (to a lesser extent) overland from Ashkabad to Mashhad. In all, 115,000 people are evacuated, 37,000 of them civilians, 18,000 children (7% of the number of Polish citizens originally exiled to the Soviet Union).<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_28" title="March 28">March 28</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/St_Nazaire_Raid" title="St Nazaire Raid">St Nazaire Raid</a> (Operation Chariot) – British Commandos raid <a href="/wiki/Saint-Nazaire" title="Saint-Nazaire">Saint-Nazaire</a> on the coast of Western France to put its dockyard facilities out of action.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/St._Mary%27s_Church,_L%C3%BCbeck" title="St. Mary's Church, Lübeck">St. Mary's Church, Lübeck</a> is destroyed by an allied bombing raid - <a href="/wiki/Bombing_of_L%C3%BCbeck_in_World_War_II" title="Bombing of Lübeck in World War II">Bombing of Lübeck in World War II</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_31" title="March 31">March 31</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Christmas_Island" title="Battle of Christmas Island">Battle of Christmas Island</a> – Japanese troops occupy <a href="/wiki/Christmas_Island" title="Christmas Island">Christmas Island</a> without resistance following a mutiny by <a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Army" title="British Indian Army">British Indian Army</a> troops against their British officers.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001,_KZ_Treblinka,_Lageplan_(Zeichnung)_II.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg/300px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg" width="300" height="186" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg/450px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg/600px-Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001%2C_KZ_Treblinka%2C_Lageplan_%28Zeichnung%29_II.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="495" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bundesarchiv_Bild_183-F0918-0201-001,_KZ_Treblinka,_Lageplan_(Zeichnung)_II.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Spring 1942: the <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi German</a> <a href="/wiki/Extermination_camp" title="Extermination camp">extermination camp</a> <a href="/wiki/Treblinka_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Treblinka II">Treblinka II</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%9345)" class="mw-redirect" title="Occupation of Poland (1939–45)">occupied Poland</a> near the village of <a href="/wiki/Treblinka,_Masovian_Voivodeship" title="Treblinka, Masovian Voivodeship">Treblinka</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li>April
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: the <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi German</a> <a href="/wiki/Extermination_camp" title="Extermination camp">extermination camp</a> <a href="/wiki/Sobib%C3%B3r_extermination_camp" title="Sobibór extermination camp">Sobibór</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%9345)" class="mw-redirect" title="Occupation of Poland (1939–45)">occupied Poland</a> on the outskirts of the town of <a href="/wiki/Sobib%C3%B3r,_Lublin_Voivodeship" title="Sobibór, Lublin Voivodeship">Sobibór</a>. Between April 1942 and October 1943, at least 160,000 people are killed here.</li>
<li>77 <a href="/wiki/Uzbeks" title="Uzbeks">Uzbek</a> prisoners of war held at <a href="/wiki/Amersfoort_concentration_camp" title="Amersfoort concentration camp">Amersfoort concentration camp</a> in the occupied Netherlands are shot by Nazi German guards, 24 of their compatriots having previously died there as a result of forced starvation.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Spring – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: the <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi German</a> <a href="/wiki/Extermination_camp" title="Extermination camp">extermination camp</a> <a href="/wiki/Treblinka_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Treblinka II">Treblinka II</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%9345)" class="mw-redirect" title="Occupation of Poland (1939–45)">occupied Poland</a> near the village of <a href="/wiki/Treblinka,_Masovian_Voivodeship" title="Treblinka, Masovian Voivodeship">Treblinka</a>. Between July 23, 1942, and October 1943, around 850,000 people are killed here,<sup id="cite_ref-Generalgouvernement.2C_2004.2C_pp._257.E2.80.93281_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Generalgouvernement.2C_2004.2C_pp._257.E2.80.93281-5">[5]</a></sup> more than 800,000 of whom are Jews.<sup id="cite_ref-CGH_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CGH-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_3" title="April 3">April 3</a> – WWII: Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on the United States and <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> troops on the <a href="/wiki/Bataan_Peninsula" class="mw-redirect" title="Bataan Peninsula">Bataan Peninsula</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_5" title="April 5">April 5</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Easter_Sunday_Raid" title="Easter Sunday Raid">Easter Sunday Raid</a> – Aircraft of the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Japanese Navy</a> attack <a href="/wiki/Colombo" title="Colombo">Colombo</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ceylon" class="mw-redirect" title="Ceylon">Ceylon</a> (<a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>). <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> <a href="/wiki/Cruisers" class="mw-redirect" title="Cruisers">cruisers</a> <a href="/wiki/HMS_Cornwall_(56)" title="HMS Cornwall (56)">HMS&#160;<i>Cornwall</i></a> and <a href="/wiki/HMS_Dorsetshire_(40)" title="HMS Dorsetshire (40)">HMS&#160;<i>Dorsetshire</i></a> are sunk southwest of the island.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_9" title="April 9">April 9</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>The Bataan Peninsula falls and the <a href="/wiki/Bataan_Death_March" title="Bataan Death March">Bataan Death March</a> begins.</li>
<li>The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on <a href="/wiki/Trincomalee" title="Trincomalee">Trincomalee</a> in Ceylon (Sri Lanka); the Royal Navy aircraft carrier <a href="/wiki/HMS_Hermes_(95)" title="HMS Hermes (95)">HMS&#160;<i>Hermes</i>&#160;(95)</a> and <a href="/wiki/Royal_Australian_Navy" title="Royal Australian Navy">Royal Australian Navy</a> destroyer <a href="/wiki/HMAS_Vampire_(D68)" title="HMAS Vampire (D68)">HMAS&#160;<i>Vampire</i></a> are sunk off the country's East Coast.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_12" title="April 12">April 12</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Bambi" title="Bambi">Disney's Bambi</a></i> was released in <a href="/wiki/Theaters" class="mw-redirect" title="Theaters">theaters</a> everywhere.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_13" title="April 13">April 13</a> – The United States <a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission" title="Federal Communications Commission">Federal Communications Commission</a>'s minimum programming time required of TV stations is cut from 15 hours to 4 hours a week during the war.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_14" title="April 14">April 14</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: The submarine <a href="/wiki/HMS_Upholder_(P37)" title="HMS Upholder (P37)">HMS&#160;<i>Upholder</i></a> is sunk.</li>
<li>WWII: The <a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-85_(1941)" title="German submarine U-85 (1941)">German submarine&#160;<i>U-85</i></a> is sunk by <a href="/wiki/USS_Roper_(DD-147)" title="USS Roper (DD-147)">USS&#160;<i>Roper</i></a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_15" title="April 15">April 15</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Award_of_the_George_Cross_to_Malta" title="Award of the George Cross to Malta">Award of the George Cross to Malta</a>: King <a href="/wiki/George_VI" title="George VI">George VI</a> awards the <a href="/wiki/George_Cross" title="George Cross">George Cross</a> to the island of <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a> to mark the <a href="/wiki/Siege_of_Malta_(World_War_II)" title="Siege of Malta (World War II)">Siege of Malta</a>, saying, "To honour her brave people I award the George Cross to the Island Fortress of Malta, to bear witness to a heroism and a devotion that will long be famous in history" (from January 1 to July 24, there is only one 24-hour period during which no bombs fall on this tiny island).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_17" title="April 17">April 17</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Henri_Giraud" title="Henri Giraud">Henri Giraud</a> the French commander captured in 1940, escapes from <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6nigstein_Fortress" title="Königstein Fortress">Königstein Fortress</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_18" title="April 18">April 18</a> – WWII: Tokyo, Japan, is attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Doolittle_Raid" title="Doolittle Raid">Doolittle Raid</a>, a small force of <a href="/wiki/B-25_Mitchell" class="mw-redirect" title="B-25 Mitchell">B-25 Mitchell</a> bomber aircraft commanded by then-Lieutenant Colonel <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Doolittle" title="Jimmy Doolittle">James "Jimmy" Doolittle</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_23" title="April 23">April 23</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: <a href="/wiki/Exeter" title="Exeter">Exeter</a> becomes the first historic English city bombed as part of the <a href="/wiki/Baedeker_Blitz" title="Baedeker Blitz">Baedeker Blitz</a> in retaliation for the British <a href="/wiki/Bombing_of_L%C3%BCbeck_in_World_War_II" title="Bombing of Lübeck in World War II">bombing of Lübeck</a>.</li>
<li>Exeter-born <a href="/wiki/William_Temple_(bishop)" title="William Temple (bishop)">William Temple</a> enthroned as <a href="/wiki/Archbishop_of_Canterbury" title="Archbishop of Canterbury">Archbishop of Canterbury</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_25" title="April 25">April 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">The Princess Elizabeth</a> registers for war service in the U.K.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_26" title="April 26">April 26</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/Reichstag_(Nazi_Germany)" title="Reichstag (Nazi Germany)">Reichstag</a> meets for the last time, dissolving itself and proclaiming <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> the "Supreme Judge of the German People", granting him the power of life and death over every German citizen.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_27" title="April 27">April 27</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: A <a href="/wiki/Conscription_Crisis_of_1944" title="Conscription Crisis of 1944">national plebiscite</a> is held in Canada on the issue of <a href="/wiki/Conscription" title="Conscription">conscription</a>.</li>
<li>The Jewish <a href="/wiki/Star_of_David" title="Star of David">Star of David</a> is required wearing for all Jews in the Netherlands and Belgium; Jews in other Nazi-controlled countries have already been wearing it.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_29" title="April 29">April 29</a> – WWII: An explosion at a chemical factory in <a href="/wiki/Tessenderlo" title="Tessenderlo">Tessenderlo</a>, Belgium leaves 200 dead and 1,000 injured.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>May – <a href="/wiki/Operation_Pluto" title="Operation Pluto">Operation Pluto</a>: The plan to construct oil pipelines under the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a> between England and France is tested in the <a href="/wiki/River_Medway" title="River Medway">River Medway</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_3" title="May 3">May 3</a>–<a href="/wiki/May_4" title="May 4">4</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Tulagi_(May_1942)" title="Invasion of Tulagi (May 1942)">Invasion of Tulagi</a> by Japanese forces in the <a href="/wiki/British_Solomon_Islands" title="British Solomon Islands">British Solomon Islands</a> of the South Pacific as part of <a href="/wiki/Operation_Mo" title="Operation Mo">Operation Mo</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_5" title="May 5">May 5</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Operation_Ironclad" class="mw-redirect" title="Operation Ironclad">Operation Ironclad</a>: British forces invade the French colony of <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_7" title="May 7">May 7</a> – WWII: On <a href="/wiki/Corregidor" title="Corregidor">Corregidor</a>, the last American and <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> forces in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> surrender to the Japanese under command of 2Lt. Robert L. Obourn (<a href="/wiki/92nd_Coast_Artillery_(United_States)" title="92nd Coast Artillery (United States)">92nd Coastal Artillery Corps Battalion</a>, G Battery) from <a href="/wiki/Fort_Mills" title="Fort Mills">Fort Mills</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ref1_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ref1-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_8" title="May 8">May 8</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Kerch_Peninsula" title="Battle of the Kerch Peninsula">Battle of the Kerch Peninsula</a>: The German <a href="/wiki/11th_Army_(Wehrmacht)" title="11th Army (Wehrmacht)">11th Army</a> begins Operation <i>Trappenjagd</i> (Bustard Hunt) and destroys the <a href="/wiki/Bridgehead" title="Bridgehead">bridgehead</a> of the three Soviet Armies (44th, 47th, and 51st) defending the <a href="/wiki/Kerch_Peninsula" title="Kerch Peninsula">Kerch Peninsula</a>, in the eastern part of the <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Coral_Sea" title="Battle of the Coral Sea">Battle of the Coral Sea</a> (first battle in naval history where 2 enemy fleets fight without seeing each other's fleets) ends in an Allied victory.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Kerch_Peninsula" title="Battle of the Kerch Peninsula">Battle of the Kerch Peninsula</a>: German and Romanian forces launches Unternehmen Trappenjagd (Operation Busted Hunt) aiming at defeating the Soviet <a href="/wiki/Crimean_Front" title="Crimean Front">Crimean Front</a> defending the <a href="/wiki/Kerch_Peninsula" title="Kerch Peninsula">Kerch Peninsula</a>. The battle ends in Axis victory. Part of the <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Front_(World_War_II)" title="Eastern Front (World War II)">Eastern Front</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_8" title="May 8">May 8</a>/<a href="/wiki/May_9" title="May 9">May 9</a> – WWII: At night, gunners of the Ceylon Garrison Artillery on Horsburgh Island in the Cocos Islands mutiny. The mutiny is crushed and three executed (the only British Commonwealth soldiers to be executed for mutiny during the Second World War).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_12" title="May 12">May 12</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Kharkov" title="Second Battle of Kharkov">Second Battle of Kharkov</a>: In the eastern <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> Army initiates a major offensive to capture the city of <a href="/wiki/Kharkov" class="mw-redirect" title="Kharkov">Kharkov</a> from the German Army, only to be encircled and destroyed.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Japanese_minelayer_Okinoshima" title="Japanese minelayer Okinoshima">Japanese minelayer&#160;<i>Okinoshima</i></a> is sunk by the American submarine <a href="/wiki/USS_S-42_(SS-153)" title="USS S-42 (SS-153)">USS&#160;<i>S-42</i></a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_14" title="May 14">May 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Copland" title="Aaron Copland">Aaron Copland</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Lincoln_Portrait" title="Lincoln Portrait">Lincoln Portrait</a></i> is performed for the first time by the <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Symphony_Orchestra" title="Cincinnati Symphony Orchestra">Cincinnati Symphony Orchestra</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_15" title="May 15">May 15</a> – WWII: In the United States, a bill creating the <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_Army_Corps" title="Women's Army Corps">Women's Auxiliary Army Corps</a> (WAAC) is signed into law.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_20" title="May 20">May 20</a> – The first African-American seamen are taken into the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a> – WWII: Mexico declares war against <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a> after the sinking of the Mexican tanker <i><a href="/wiki/Faja_de_Oro" class="mw-redirect" title="Faja de Oro">Faja de Oro</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-160_(1941)" title="German submarine U-160 (1941)">German submarine&#160;<i>U-160</i></a> off <a href="/wiki/Key_West" title="Key West">Key West</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Bir_Hakeim" title="Battle of Bir Hakeim">Battle of Bir Hakeim</a>: The Free French and British troops slow the German advance in North Africa.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Anglo-Soviet_Treaty_of_1942" title="Anglo-Soviet Treaty of 1942">Anglo-Soviet Treaty of 1942</a> to help establish military and political alliance between the <a href="/wiki/USSR" class="mw-redirect" title="USSR">USSR</a> and the <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> is signed in London by foreign Secretary <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Eden" title="Anthony Eden">Anthony Eden</a> and by Soviet foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Vyacheslav_Molotov" title="Vyacheslav Molotov">Vyacheslav Molotov</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Operation_Anthropoid" title="Operation Anthropoid">Operation Anthropoid</a>: Czech paratroopers attempt to assassinate <a href="/wiki/Reinhard_Heydrich" title="Reinhard Heydrich">Reinhard Heydrich</a> in <a href="/wiki/Prague" title="Prague">Prague</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_30" title="May 30">May 30</a>–<a href="/wiki/May_31" title="May 31">31</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Bombing_of_Cologne_in_World_War_II" title="Bombing of Cologne in World War II">Bombing of Cologne</a> – British <a href="/wiki/RAF_Bomber_Command" title="RAF Bomber Command">RAF Bomber Command</a>'s "Operation Millennium", its first 1,000 bomber raid, with associated fires make 13,000 families homeless and kills around 475 people, mostly civilians; 3,330 non-residential buildings are totally destroyed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_31" title="May 31">May 31</a>–<a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Attack_on_Sydney_Harbour" title="Attack on Sydney Harbour">Attack on Sydney Harbour</a>: Japanese <a href="/wiki/Midget_submarine" title="Midget submarine">midget submarines</a> infiltrate Sydney Harbour in Australia in an attempt to attack Allied warships.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hiryu_f075712.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Hiryu_f075712.jpg/300px-Hiryu_f075712.jpg" width="300" height="223" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Hiryu_f075712.jpg/450px-Hiryu_f075712.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/Hiryu_f075712.jpg/600px-Hiryu_f075712.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5024" data-file-height="3740" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hiryu_f075712.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
June 4: The Japanese aircraft carrier, <a href="/wiki/Japanese_aircraft_carrier_Hiry%C5%AB" title="Japanese aircraft carrier Hiryū"><i>Hiryū</i></a> under attack by US aircraft at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Midway" title="Battle of Midway">Battle of Midway</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: Mexico declares war on Germany, Italy and Japan.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Grand_Coulee_Dam" title="Grand Coulee Dam">Grand Coulee Dam</a> is finished on the <a href="/wiki/Columbia_River" title="Columbia River">Columbia River</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_4" title="June 4">June 4</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Reinhard_Heydrich" title="Reinhard Heydrich">Reinhard Heydrich</a> succumbs to wounds sustained on <a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a> from Czechoslovakian paratroopers acting in <a href="/wiki/Operation_Anthropoid" title="Operation Anthropoid">Operation Anthropoid</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_5" title="June 5">June 5</a> – The United States declares war on <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a> &amp; <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_4" title="June 4">June 4</a>–<a href="/wiki/June_7" title="June 7">June 7</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Midway" title="Battle of Midway">Battle of Midway</a>: The Japanese naval advance in the Pacific is halted.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_7" title="June 7">June 7</a> – WWII: Japanese forces invade the <a href="/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a> (the first invasion of American soil in 128 years).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_8" title="June 8">June 8</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Attack_on_Sydney_Harbour" title="Attack on Sydney Harbour">Attack on Sydney Harbour</a>: The Australian cities of Sydney and <a href="/wiki/Newcastle,_New_South_Wales" title="Newcastle, New South Wales">Newcastle</a> are shelled by Japanese submarines. The eastern suburbs of both cities are damaged and the east coast is blacked out.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_9" title="June 9">June 9</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nazism" title="Nazism">Nazis</a> burn the Czech village of <a href="/wiki/Lidice" title="Lidice">Lidice</a> in reprisal for the killing of <a href="/wiki/Reinhard_Heydrich" title="Reinhard Heydrich">Reinhard Heydrich</a>.</li>
<li>(12:30&#160;a.m.) – B-17 <a href="/wiki/Flying_Fortress" class="mw-redirect" title="Flying Fortress">Flying Fortress</a> air crash near <a href="/wiki/Auckland" title="Auckland">Auckland</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_10" title="June 10">June 10</a> – WWII: The Gestapo massacres 173 male residents of <a href="/wiki/Lidice" title="Lidice">Lidice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a> in retaliation for the killing of <a href="/wiki/Reinhard_Heydrich" title="Reinhard Heydrich">Reinhard Heydrich</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_12" title="June 12">June 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: On her 13th birthday, <a href="/wiki/Anne_Frank" title="Anne Frank">Anne Frank</a> makes the first entry in her new <a href="/wiki/The_Diary_of_a_Young_Girl" title="The Diary of a Young Girl">diary</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_13" title="June 13">June 13</a> – WWII: The United States opens its <a href="/wiki/Office_of_War_Information" class="mw-redirect" title="Office of War Information">Office of War Information</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Propaganda" title="Propaganda">propaganda</a> center.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_18" title="June 18">June 18</a> – WWII: The SS surrounds the church where <a href="/wiki/Jan_Kubi%C5%A1" title="Jan Kubiš">Jan Kubiš</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jozef_Gab%C4%8D%C3%ADk" title="Jozef Gabčík">Jozef Gabčík</a>, the assassins of <a href="/wiki/Reinhard_Heydrich" title="Reinhard Heydrich">Reinhard Heydrich</a>, are hiding. Kubiš is fatally wounded in the ensuing shootout and Gabčík commits suicide to avoid capture.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_23" title="June 23">June 23</a> – The experimental early type of a nuclear reactor L-IV led to <a href="/wiki/Leipzig_L-IV_experiment_accident" title="Leipzig L-IV experiment accident">an accident</a>, becoming the first nuclear accident in history and consisting of steam explosion and reactor fire in <a href="/wiki/Leipzig" title="Leipzig">Leipzig</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_28" title="June 28">June 28</a> – WWII: The Germans launch <a href="/wiki/Case_Blue" title="Case Blue">Case Blue</a>, Army Group South's drive to Stalingrad and the Baku Oil fields.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_29" title="June 29">June 29</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/11th_Army_(Wehrmacht)" title="11th Army (Wehrmacht)">German Eleventh Army</a> under <a href="/wiki/Erich_von_Manstein" title="Erich von Manstein">Erich von Manstein</a> takes <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, although fighting rages until <a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>July – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: Inmates of <a href="/wiki/Westerbork_transit_camp" title="Westerbork transit camp">Westerbork transit camp</a> in the occupied <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> begin to be shipped to Nazi <a href="/wiki/Extermination_camp" title="Extermination camp">extermination camps</a>. From now until 1944 around 107,000, mostly Jewish, from here will be killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_1" title="July 1">July 1</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_27" title="July 27">July 27</a> – WWII: The <a href="/wiki/First_Battle_of_El_Alamein" title="First Battle of El Alamein">First Battle of El Alamein</a>: British forces prevent a second advance by Axis forces into Egypt.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_3" title="July 3">July 3</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a>, occupied only by aborigines, falls to the Japanese Naval construction force deployed to construct an air field on the island.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_4" title="July 4">July 4</a> – WWII in the <a href="/wiki/European_Theater_of_Operations" class="mw-redirect" title="European Theater of Operations">European Theater of Operations</a>:
<ul>
<li>Twenty-four ships are sunk by German bombers and submarines after <a href="/wiki/Convoy_PQ_17" title="Convoy PQ 17">Convoy PQ 17</a> to the Soviet Union is scattered in the Arctic Ocean to evade the <a href="/wiki/German_battleship_Tirpitz" title="German battleship Tirpitz">German battleship <i>Tirpitz</i></a>.</li>
<li>The United States <a href="/wiki/Eighth_Air_Force" title="Eighth Air Force">Eighth Air Force</a> inauspiciously flies its first mission in Europe using borrowed British planes and bombs targets in the Netherlands, such as De Kooy airfield attached to <a href="/wiki/Den_Helder" title="Den Helder">Den Helder</a> naval base. Three of six aircraft return;<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> For this mission, Captain Charles C. Kegelman is the first member of the Force to be awarded the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Distinguished_Flying_Cross_(United_States)" title="Distinguished Flying Cross (United States)">Distinguished Flying Cross</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_6" title="July 6">July 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: <a href="/wiki/Anne_Frank" title="Anne Frank">Anne Frank</a>'s family goes into hiding in an attic above her father's office in an <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> warehouse.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_8" title="July 8">July 8</a> – Turkish prime minister <a href="/wiki/Refik_Saydam" title="Refik Saydam">Refik Saydam</a> dies while working in office. For one day he is succeeded by <a href="/wiki/Ahmet_Fikri_T%C3%BCzer" title="Ahmet Fikri Tüzer">Ahmet Fikri Tüzer</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/%C5%9E%C3%BCkr%C3%BC_Saraco%C4%9Flu" title="Şükrü Saracoğlu">Şükrü Saracoğlu</a> forms the new (13th) government in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_13" title="July 13">July 13</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sink 3 more merchant ships in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_St._Lawrence" class="mw-redirect" title="Gulf of St. Lawrence">Gulf of St. Lawrence</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_14" title="July 14">July 14</a> – WWII: Germany introduces the <a href="/wiki/Ostvolk_Medal" title="Ostvolk Medal">Ostvolk Medal</a> for Soviet personnel in the <a href="/wiki/Wehrmacht" title="Wehrmacht">Wehrmacht</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_16" title="July 16">July 16</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: By order of the <a href="/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a> government headed by <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Laval" title="Pierre Laval">Pierre Laval</a>, French police officers round-up 13,000–20,000 Jews and imprison them in the <a href="/wiki/Winter_Velodrome" class="mw-redirect" title="Winter Velodrome">Winter Velodrome</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Georges_B%C3%A9gu%C3%A9" title="Georges Bégué">Georges Bégué</a> and others escape from the <a href="/wiki/Mauzac,_Haute-Garonne" title="Mauzac, Haute-Garonne">Mauzac</a> prison camp.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_18" title="July 18">July 18</a> – WWII: The Germans test fly the <a href="/wiki/Messerschmitt_Me_262" title="Messerschmitt Me 262">Messerschmitt Me 262</a> (using only its <a href="/wiki/Jet_engine" title="Jet engine">jet engines</a>) for the first time.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_19" title="July 19">July 19</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Atlantic" title="Battle of the Atlantic">Battle of the Atlantic</a>: German Grand Admiral <a href="/wiki/Karl_D%C3%B6nitz" title="Karl Dönitz">Karl Dönitz</a> orders the last <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> to withdraw from their United States Atlantic coast positions, in response to an effective American convoy system.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_21" title="July 21">July 21</a> – WWII: The Japanese establish a beachhead on the north coast of <a href="/wiki/New_Guinea" title="New Guinea">New Guinea</a> in the Buna-Gona area; a small Australian force begins a rearguard action on the <a href="/wiki/Kokoda_Track_campaign" title="Kokoda Track campaign">Kokoda Track campaign</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_22" title="July 22">July 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: The systematic deportation of Jews from the <a href="/wiki/Warsaw_Ghetto" title="Warsaw Ghetto">Warsaw Ghetto</a> begins.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_23" title="July 23">July 23</a> – The Holocaust: The <a href="/wiki/Gas_chamber" title="Gas chamber">gas chambers</a> at <a href="/wiki/Treblinka_extermination_camp" title="Treblinka extermination camp">Treblinka extermination camp</a> begin operation, killing 6,500 Jews newly arrived from the Warsaw Ghetto.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_29" title="July 29">July 29</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Presidium_of_the_Supreme_Soviet" title="Presidium of the Supreme Soviet">Presidium of the Supreme Soviet</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> institutes the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Suvorov" title="Order of Suvorov">Order of Suvorov</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Kutuzov" title="Order of Kutuzov">Order of Kutuzov</a>, and reinstates the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Alexander_Nevsky" title="Order of Alexander Nevsky">Order of Alexander Nevsky</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_30" title="July 30">July 30</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/WAVES" title="WAVES">WAVES</a> (Women Accepted for Volunteer Emergency Service), the United States Naval Reserve (Women's Reserve), is signed into law.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/SS_Robert_E._Lee_(1924)" class="mw-redirect" title="SS Robert E. Lee (1924)">SS <i>Robert E. Lee</i></a> sunk in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a> by <a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-166_(1941)" title="German submarine U-166 (1941)"><i>U-166</i></a> which is itself sunk by the escorting patrol craft.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_31" title="July 31">July 31</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Oxford_Committee_for_Famine_Relief" class="mw-redirect" title="Oxford Committee for Famine Relief">Oxford Committee for Famine Relief</a> (Oxfam) is founded in England.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_7" title="August 7">August 7</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal_Campaign" title="Guadalcanal Campaign">Guadalcanal Campaign</a> begins – The <a href="/wiki/U.S._Navy" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Navy">U.S. Navy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Marine_Corps" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Marine Corps">U.S. Marine Corps</a> begin the first American offensive of the war with an <a href="/wiki/Amphibious_warfare" title="Amphibious warfare">amphibious</a> landing on the island of <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Solomon_Islands" title="Solomon Islands">Solomon Islands</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_8" title="August 8">August 8</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: Allied North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_SC_94" title="Convoy SC 94">convoy SC 94</a> loses ten ships as the first to be heavily attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> resuming mid-Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Wolfpack_(naval_tactic)" title="Wolfpack (naval tactic)">wolf pack</a> attacks through the climactic winter of 1942/43.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
<li>WWII: In Washington, D.C., six German <a href="/wiki/Sabotage" title="Sabotage">saboteurs</a> are executed for their role in a failed mission of <a href="/wiki/Operation_Pastorius" title="Operation Pastorius">Operation Pastorius</a>. (Two others are cooperative and receive sentences of life imprisonment instead, being freed a few years after the end of the war.)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_9" title="August 9">August 9</a>
<ul>
<li>Indian leader, <a href="/wiki/Mohandas_Gandhi" class="mw-redirect" title="Mohandas Gandhi">Mohandas Gandhi</a> is arrested in <a href="/wiki/Bombay" class="mw-redirect" title="Bombay">Bombay</a> by British forces.</li>
<li><i>Start</i>, led by the goalkeeper Nikolai Trusevich, <a href="/wiki/The_Death_Match" title="The Death Match">play football against the German Luftwaffe team Flakelf in Nazi-occupied Kiev</a>. Against all odds, they win 5–3. Eight of them are later arrested and tortured, and at least four are killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Leningrad_premi%C3%A8re_of_Shostakovich%27s_Symphony_No._7" title="Leningrad première of Shostakovich's Symphony No. 7">Leningrad première of Shostakovich's Symphony No. 7</a> with the city still under siege.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_13" title="August 13">August 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Quit_India" class="mw-redirect" title="Quit India">Quit India</a> resolution is passed by the <a href="/wiki/Bombay" class="mw-redirect" title="Bombay">Bombay</a> session of the All India Congress Committee (AICC), which leads to the start of a historical civil disobedience movement across India.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_15" title="August 15">August 15</a> – WWII: The American tanker <a href="/wiki/SS_Ohio" title="SS Ohio"><i>Ohio</i></a> reaches Malta as part of the convoy of <i><a href="/wiki/Operation_Pedestal" title="Operation Pedestal">Operation Pedestal</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_16" title="August 16">August 16</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Polish-Jewish" class="mw-redirect" title="Polish-Jewish">Polish-Jewish</a> teacher <a href="/wiki/Janusz_Korczak" title="Janusz Korczak">Janusz Korczak</a> follows a group of Jewish children into the <a href="/wiki/Treblinka_extermination_camp" title="Treblinka extermination camp">Treblinka extermination camp</a>.</li>
<li>U.S. Navy blimp <i><a href="/wiki/L_class_blimp" class="mw-redirect" title="L class blimp">L-8</a></i> (Flight 101) comes ashore near San Francisco, eventually coming down in <a href="/wiki/Daly_City,_California" title="Daly City, California">Daly City</a> (the crew is missing).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_17" title="August 17">August 17</a> – WWII: First raid by heavy bombers of U.S. <a href="/wiki/Eighth_Air_Force" title="Eighth Air Force">Eighth Air Force</a> based in England against occupied France.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_19" title="August 19">August 19</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Dieppe_Raid" title="Dieppe Raid">Dieppe Raid</a>: Allied forces raid <a href="/wiki/Dieppe" title="Dieppe">Dieppe</a>, France.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_20" title="August 20">August 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Plutonium" title="Plutonium">Plutonium</a> is isolated for the first time at the <a href="/wiki/Metallurgical_Laboratory" title="Metallurgical Laboratory">Metallurgical Laboratory</a> of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Chicago" title="University of Chicago">University of Chicago</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_21" title="August 21">August 21</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Tenaru" title="Battle of the Tenaru">Battle of the Tenaru</a>: Allies defeat Japanese land forces on <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_22" title="August 22">August 22</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Vargas_Era#World_War_II" title="Vargas Era">Brazil declares war</a> on Germany and Italy.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_23" title="August 23">August 23</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a> begins: <a href="/wiki/Case_Blue" title="Case Blue">German troops</a> reach the suburbs of <a href="/wiki/Stalingrad" class="mw-redirect" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_24" title="August 24">August 24</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: <a href="/wiki/Charge_of_the_Savoia_Cavalleria_at_Isbuscenskij" class="mw-redirect" title="Charge of the Savoia Cavalleria at Isbuscenskij">Charge of the Savoia Cavalleria at Isbuscenskij</a>: An Italian <a href="/wiki/Cavalry" title="Cavalry">cavalry</a> regiment attacks Soviet forces with drawn <a href="/wiki/Sabre" title="Sabre">sabres</a> at Isbuscenskij in Russia, one of the last major cavalry <a href="/wiki/Charge_(warfare)" title="Charge (warfare)">charges</a>.</li>
<li>WWII: Allied North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_ON_122" title="Convoy ON 122">convoy ON 122</a> is attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> which sink four ships.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li>WWII: 2-day <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Eastern_Solomons" title="Battle of the Eastern Solomons">Battle of the Eastern Solomons</a> opens: Bombers from carrier <a href="/wiki/USS_Saratoga_(CV-3)" title="USS Saratoga (CV-3)">USS <i>Saratoga</i></a> sink <a href="/wiki/Japanese_aircraft_carrier_Ry%C5%ABj%C5%8D" title="Japanese aircraft carrier Ryūjō">Japanese aircraft carrier <i>Ryūjō</i></a> near <a href="/wiki/Santa_Isabel_Island" title="Santa Isabel Island">Santa Isabel Island</a>, helping to lead to an Allied victory.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney" title="Walt Disney">Walt Disney</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Live-action_animated_film" title="Live-action animated film">live-action animated film</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Saludos_Amigos" title="Saludos Amigos">Saludos Amigos</a></i> has its world premiere in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_25" title="August 25">August 25</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Milne_Bay" title="Battle of Milne Bay">Battle of Milne Bay</a> opens when Japanese <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">marines</a> land at <a href="/wiki/Milne_Bay" title="Milne Bay">Milne Bay</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prince_George,_Duke_of_Kent" title="Prince George, Duke of Kent">Prince George, Duke of Kent</a>, brother to King <a href="/wiki/George_VI" title="George VI">George VI</a> and King <a href="/wiki/Edward_VIII" title="Edward VIII">Edward VIII</a>, dies in a flying accident over <a href="/wiki/Morven,_Caithness" title="Morven, Caithness">Morven</a> in Scotland at the age of 39.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_27" title="August 27">August 27</a>–<a href="/wiki/August_28" title="August 28">28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sarny_Massacre" title="Sarny Massacre">Sarny Massacre</a>: Nazi troops and the <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Auxiliary_Police" title="Ukrainian Auxiliary Police">Ukrainian Auxiliary Police</a> systematically execute more than 14,000 people, mostly Jews, in and around <a href="/wiki/Sarny" title="Sarny">Sarny</a> in <a href="/wiki/History_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%931945)" title="History of Poland (1939–1945)">German-occupied Poland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_30" title="August 30">August 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a> is formally annexed to the German Reich.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_30" title="August 30">August 30</a>–<a href="/wiki/September_5" title="September 5">September 5</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Alam_el_Halfa" title="Battle of Alam el Halfa">Battle of Alam el Halfa</a> – British forces in the Western Desert resist German attack.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_31" title="August 31">August 31</a> – <a href="/wiki/1942_Luxembourgish_general_strike" title="1942 Luxembourgish general strike">1942 Luxembourgish general strike</a> is launched to protest against forced conscription in Luxembourg.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_2" title="September 2">September 2</a> – The island of <a href="/wiki/Les_Casquets" title="Les Casquets">Les Casquets</a> in the Channel Islands is raided by the forerunner of the British <a href="/wiki/Special_Air_Service" title="Special Air Service">SAS</a>, the <a href="/wiki/SSRF" class="mw-redirect" title="SSRF">SSRF</a>, led by Major <a href="/wiki/Gus_March-Phillipps" title="Gus March-Phillipps">Gus March-Phillipps</a>; this is one of the first raids by <a href="/wiki/Anders_Lassen" title="Anders Lassen">Anders Lassen</a> VC. In the raid the entire garrison of 7 is abducted and returned to England as prisoners and the radio and lighthouse wrecked.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_3" title="September 3">September 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: A German attempt to liquidate the Jewish <a href="/wiki/%C5%81achwa_Ghetto" title="Łachwa Ghetto">Łachwa Ghetto</a> in <a href="/wiki/Occupation_of_Poland_(1939%E2%80%9345)" class="mw-redirect" title="Occupation of Poland (1939–45)">occupied Poland</a> leads to an uprising, probably the first <a href="/wiki/Ghetto_uprising" title="Ghetto uprising">ghetto uprising</a> of the war.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_5" title="September 5">September 5</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Milne_Bay" title="Battle of Milne Bay">Battle of Milne Bay</a>: Japanese forces suffer their first defeat on land.</li>
<li>The Holocaust: The Jews of <a href="/wiki/Wolbrom" title="Wolbrom">Wolbrom</a> in occupied Poland are rounded up by the Germans and their Ukrainian collaborators. What was once a flourishing community suddenly ceases to exist.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_9" title="September 9">September 9</a> – WWII: A Japanese <a href="/wiki/Floatplane" title="Floatplane">floatplane</a> drops <a href="/wiki/Incendiary_device" title="Incendiary device">incendiary devices</a> at <a href="/wiki/Mount_Emily" title="Mount Emily">Mount Emily</a>, near <a href="/wiki/Brookings,_Oregon" title="Brookings, Oregon">Brookings, Oregon</a>, in the first of two "<a href="/wiki/Lookout_Air_Raids" title="Lookout Air Raids">Lookout Air Raids</a>", the first bombing of the continental United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_10" title="September 10">September 10</a>
<ul>
<li>WWII: North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_ON_127" title="Convoy ON 127">convoy ON 127</a> is attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a>, sinking six ships.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Women_Airforce_Service_Pilots" title="Women Airforce Service Pilots">Women's Auxiliary Ferrying Squadron</a> (WAFS) begins operation in the United States.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_12" title="September 12">September 12</a> – The <a href="/wiki/RMS_Laconia" title="RMS Laconia">RMS&#160;<i>Laconia</i></a>, carrying civilians, Allied soldiers and Italian Prisoners of War, is torpedoed off the coast of West Africa and sinks, killing 1,649 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_15" title="September 15">September 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_Flying_Training_Detachment" title="Women's Flying Training Detachment">Women's Flying Training Detachment</a> (WFTD) established in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9e_Borrel" title="Andrée Borrel">Andrée Borrel</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lise_de_Baissac" title="Lise de Baissac">Lise de Baissac</a> become the first female <a href="/wiki/Special_Operations_Executive" title="Special Operations Executive">SOE</a> agents to be parachuted into occupied France.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_26" title="September 26">September 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: Nazi official <a href="/wiki/August_Frank" title="August Frank">August Frank</a> issues the <a href="/wiki/August_Frank_memorandum" title="August Frank memorandum">August Frank memorandum</a> setting out how the belongings of "evacuated" (i.e. murdered) Jews are to be disposed of.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a> – WWII: Both <a href="/wiki/Commerce_raiding" title="Commerce raiding">commerce raiding</a> <a href="/wiki/German_auxiliary_cruiser_Stier" title="German auxiliary cruiser Stier">German auxiliary cruiser <i>Stier</i></a> and American <a href="/wiki/Liberty_ship" title="Liberty ship">Liberty ship</a> <a href="/wiki/SS_Stephen_Hopkins" title="SS Stephen Hopkins">SS&#160;<i>Stephen Hopkins</i></a> sink following a gun battle in the South Atlantic. <i>Hilfskreuzer</i> <i>Stier</i> is the only commerce raider to be sunk by a <a href="/wiki/Defensively_equipped_merchant_ship" title="Defensively equipped merchant ship">defensively equipped merchant ship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_29" title="September 29">September 29</a> – WWII at <a href="/wiki/Babi_Yar" title="Babi Yar">Babi Yar</a> a ravine in <a href="/wiki/Kiev" title="Kiev">Kiev</a>, 33,771 Jews are killed during a two-day massacre.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_2" title="October 2">October 2</a> – The British cruiser <a href="/wiki/HMS_Curacoa_(D41)" title="HMS Curacoa (D41)">HMS&#160;<i>Curacoa</i></a> collides with the liner <a href="/wiki/RMS_Queen_Mary" title="RMS Queen Mary">RMS&#160;<i>Queen Mary</i></a> (carrying troops from the United States) off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Donegal" title="Donegal">Donegal</a> and sinks; 338 drown.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_3" title="October 3">October 3</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/V-2_rocket" title="V-2 rocket">A-4 rocket</a> is successfully launched from <a href="/wiki/Test_Stand_VII" title="Test Stand VII">Test Stand VII</a> at <a href="/wiki/Peenem%C3%BCnde" title="Peenemünde">Peenemünde</a>, Germany. The rocket flies 147 kilometres wide and reaches a height of 84.5 kilometres, becoming the first man-made object to reach space.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_9" title="October 9">October 9</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Westminster_Adoption_Act_1942" title="Statute of Westminster Adoption Act 1942">Statute of Westminster Adoption Act</a> passed by the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Australia" title="Parliament of Australia">Parliament of Australia</a> formalizes Australian autonomy from the United Kingdom.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_11" title="October 11">October 11</a> – WWII – <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Cape_Esperance" title="Battle of Cape Esperance">Battle of Cape Esperance</a>: On the northwest coast of <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> ships intercept and defeat a Japanese fleet on their way to reinforce troops on the island.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a> – WWII: North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_SC_104" title="Convoy SC 104">convoy SC 104</a> is attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sinking seven ships.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_14" title="October 14">October 14</a> – A <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boat</a> sinks the ferry <a href="/wiki/SS_Caribou" title="SS Caribou">SS&#160;<i>Caribou</i></a> off <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_(island)" title="Newfoundland (island)">Newfoundland</a>, killing 137.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_16" title="October 16">October 16</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Hurricane" class="mw-redirect" title="Hurricane">hurricane</a> and flood in <a href="/wiki/Bengal" title="Bengal">Bengal</a> kill 40,000.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources"><span title="Which storm? (March 2017)">specify</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_Mouse_of_Tomorrow&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The Mouse of Tomorrow (page does not exist)">The Mouse of Tomorrow</a></i> featuring the debut of <a href="/wiki/Mighty_Mouse" title="Mighty Mouse">Mighty Mouse</a> is released.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_18" title="October 18">October 18</a> – WWII – Hitler issues <a href="/wiki/Commando_Order" title="Commando Order">Commando Order</a> which stipulates that all Allied <a href="/wiki/Commando" title="Commando">commandos</a> encountered by German forces should be executed immediately without trial, even in proper uniforms, in response to the <a href="/wiki/Dieppe_Raid" title="Dieppe Raid">Dieppe Raid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Operation_Basalt" title="Operation Basalt">Operation Basalt</a> conducted by the Allies. After the war, the <a href="/wiki/Nuremberg_trials" title="Nuremberg trials">Nuremberg trials</a> found this order a direct violation of the <a href="/wiki/Laws_and_customs_of_war" class="mw-redirect" title="Laws and customs of war">laws and customs of war</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_21" title="October 21">October 21</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Royal_New_Zealand_Air_Force" title="Royal New Zealand Air Force">Royal New Zealand Air Force</a> <a href="/wiki/Torpedo_Bomber" class="mw-redirect" title="Torpedo Bomber">Torpedo Bomber</a> sinks the German <a href="/wiki/MS_Palatia_(1928)" title="MS Palatia (1928)">MS Palatia (1928)</a> with a loss of 946 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a> – Award-winning composer and songwriter <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Rainger" title="Ralph Rainger">Ralph Rainger</a> ("Thanks for the Memory") is among 12 people killed in the mid-air collision between an <a href="/wiki/American_Airlines" title="American Airlines">American Airlines</a> <a href="/wiki/DC-3" class="mw-redirect" title="DC-3">DC-3</a> airliner and a U.S. Army bomber near <a href="/wiki/Palm_Springs,_California" title="Palm Springs, California">Palm Springs, California</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a>–<a href="/wiki/October_26" title="October 26">26</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_for_Henderson_Field" title="Battle for Henderson Field">Battle for Henderson Field</a>: Japanese forces fail to recapture <a href="/wiki/Honiara_International_Airport" title="Honiara International Airport">Henderson Field</a> airfield in <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a> from the Americans.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a>–<a href="/wiki/November_4" title="November 4">November 4</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_El_Alamein" title="Second Battle of El Alamein">Second Battle of El Alamein</a>: British troops go on the offensive against the Axis forces.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_26" title="October 26">October 26</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Santa_Cruz_Islands" title="Battle of the Santa Cruz Islands">Battle of the Santa Cruz Islands</a>: Two Japanese aircraft carriers are heavily damaged and one U.S. Navy carrier is sunk.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_28" title="October 28">October 28</a>
<ul>
<li>Film actor <a href="/wiki/Errol_Flynn" title="Errol Flynn">Errol Flynn</a> is accused of statutory rape by two teenage girls.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Alaska_Highway" title="Alaska Highway">Alaska Highway</a> is completed.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_29" title="October 29">October 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: In the United Kingdom, leading clergymen and political figures hold a public meeting to register outrage over <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a>'s persecution of Jews.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_30" title="October 30">October 30</a> – WWII:
<ul>
