<li><a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sink eleven ships attacking diversionary <a href="/wiki/Convoy_SL_125" title="Convoy SL 125">convoy SL 125</a>, but move out of the path of approaching <a href="/wiki/Troopship" title="Troopship">troopships</a> carrying Allied <a href="/wiki/Operation_Torch" title="Operation Torch">Operation Torch</a> invasion forces.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li>British sailors board <a href="/wiki/German_submarine_U-559" title="German submarine U-559"><i>U-559</i></a> as it sinks in the Mediterranean and retrieve its <a href="/wiki/Enigma_machine" title="Enigma machine">Enigma machine</a> and codebooks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_1" title="November 1">November 1</a> – WWII: North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_SC_107" title="Convoy SC 107">convoy SC 107</a> is heavily attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sinking fifteen ships.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_2" title="November 2">November 2</a> – A <a href="/wiki/USAAF" class="mw-redirect" title="USAAF">USAAF</a> squadron, including <a href="/wiki/B-24_Liberator" class="mw-redirect" title="B-24 Liberator">B-24 Liberators</a>, intercepts many <a href="/wiki/Luftwaffe" title="Luftwaffe">Luftwaffe</a> patrols off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Oran,_Algeria" class="mw-redirect" title="Oran, Algeria">Oran, Algeria</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_3" title="November 3">November 3</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_El_Alamein" title="Second Battle of El Alamein">Second Battle of El Alamein</a>: German forces under <a href="/wiki/Erwin_Rommel" title="Erwin Rommel">Erwin Rommel</a> are forced to retreat during the night.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_8" title="November 8">November 8</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Operation_Torch" title="Operation Torch">Operation Torch</a>: United States and United Kingdom forces land in <a href="/wiki/French_North_Africa" title="French North Africa">French North Africa</a>.</li>
<li>French Resistance Coup in <a href="/wiki/Algiers" title="Algiers">Algiers</a>: 400 French civil resisters neutralize the Vichyist XIXth Army Corps and the Vichyist generals (Juin, Darlan, etc.) thus allowing the immediate success of Operation Torch in Algiers, and ultimately the whole of <a href="/wiki/French_North_Africa" title="French North Africa">French North Africa</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_9" title="November 9">November 9</a> – WWII: U.S serviceman <a href="/wiki/Edward_Leonski" class="mw-redirect" title="Edward Leonski">Edward Leonski</a> is hanged at Melbourne's Pentridge Prison for the "Brown-Out" murders of three women in May.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_10" title="November 10">November 10</a> – WWII: In violation of a <a href="/wiki/1940" title="1940">1940</a> armistice, Germany invades <a href="/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a>, following French Admiral <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Darlan" title="François Darlan">François Darlan</a>'s agreement to an armistice with the <a href="/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="Allies of World War II">Allies</a> in <a href="/wiki/North_Africa" title="North Africa">North Africa</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_12" title="November 12">November 12</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal_Campaign" title="Guadalcanal Campaign">Guadalcanal Campaign</a>: A naval battle near <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a> starts between Japanese and American forces.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_13" title="November 13">November 13</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal_Campaign" title="Guadalcanal Campaign">Guadalcanal Campaign</a>: Aviators from the <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(CV-6)" title="USS Enterprise (CV-6)">USS&#160;<i>Enterprise</i></a> sink the Japanese <a href="/wiki/Battleship" title="Battleship">battleship</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Japanese_battleship_Hiei" title="Japanese battleship Hiei">Hiei</a></i>.</li>
<li>British forces capture <a href="/wiki/Tobruk" title="Tobruk">Tobruk</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_15" title="November 15">November 15</a> – WWII:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Naval_Battle_of_Guadalcanal" title="Naval Battle of Guadalcanal">Naval Battle of Guadalcanal</a> ends: Although the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> suffers heavy losses, it retains control of <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal" title="Guadalcanal">Guadalcanal</a>.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/BOAC" class="mw-redirect" title="BOAC">BOAC</a> scheduled passenger flight, a <a href="/wiki/DC-3" class="mw-redirect" title="DC-3">DC-3</a> with registration G-AGBB, (formerly <a href="/wiki/KLM" title="KLM">KLM</a> PH-ALI, Ibis), en route between <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bristol" title="Bristol">Bristol</a>, is attacked over the <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Biscay" title="Bay of Biscay">Bay of Biscay</a> by German fighters. Although damaged, it escapes and lands in England. Other attacks follow on the same aircraft and scheduled route: <a href="/wiki/April_19" title="April 19">April 19</a> and <a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a>, <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a> (fatal).</li>
<li>British forces capture <a href="/wiki/Derna,_Libya" title="Derna, Libya">Derna, Libya</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_18" title="November 18">November 18</a> – WWII: North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_ON_144" title="Convoy ON 144">convoy ON 144</a> is attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sinking five ships.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_19" title="November 19">November 19</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a>: <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> forces under General <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Zhukov" title="Georgy Zhukov">Georgy Zhukov</a> launch the <a href="/wiki/Operation_Uranus" title="Operation Uranus">Operation Uranus</a> counter-attacks at <a href="/wiki/Stalingrad" class="mw-redirect" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a>, turning the tide of the battle in the USSR's favor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_20" title="November 20">November 20</a> – WWII: British forces capture <a href="/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_21" title="November 21">November 21</a> – The completion of the <a href="/wiki/Alaska_Highway" title="Alaska Highway">Alaska Highway</a> (also known as the Alcan Highway) is celebrated (however, the "<a href="/wiki/Highway" title="Highway">highway</a>" is not usable by general vehicles until <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_22" title="November 22">November 22</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a>: The situation for the German attackers of <a href="/wiki/Stalingrad" class="mw-redirect" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> seems desperate during the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> counter-attack <a href="/wiki/Operation_Uranus" title="Operation Uranus">Operation Uranus</a>, and General <a href="/wiki/Friedrich_Paulus" title="Friedrich Paulus">Friedrich Paulus</a> sends <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> a <a href="/wiki/Telegram" class="mw-redirect" title="Telegram">telegram</a> saying that the <a href="/wiki/6th_Army_(Wehrmacht)" title="6th Army (Wehrmacht)">German Sixth Army</a> is surrounded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_23" title="November 23">November 23</a> – WWII
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boat</a> sinks the SS <i>Ben Lomond</i> off the coast of Brazil. One crewman, Chinese second steward <a href="/wiki/Poon_Lim" title="Poon Lim">Poon Lim</a>, is separated from the others and spends 130 days adrift until he is rescued on <a href="/wiki/April_3" title="April 3">April 3</a>, <a href="/wiki/1943" title="1943">1943</a>.</li>
<li>Legislation approves the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">United States Coast Guard</a> Women's Reserve to help fill jobs and free men to serve during the war effort. They are known as the <a href="/wiki/SPARS" title="SPARS">SPARS</a> ("Semper Paratus, Always Ready!")</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_25" title="November 25">November 25</a>–<a href="/wiki/November_26" title="November 26">26</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Operation_Harling" title="Operation Harling">Operation Harling</a>: A British <a href="/wiki/Special_Operations_Executive" title="Special Operations Executive">Special Operations Executive</a> team, together with <a href="/wiki/Greek_Resistance" title="Greek Resistance">Greek Resistance</a> fighters, blows up the <a href="/wiki/Gorgopotamos" title="Gorgopotamos">Gorgopotamos</a> viaduct in the first major sabotage act in occupied continental Europe.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_26" title="November 26">November 26</a> – The movie <i><a href="/wiki/Casablanca_(film)" title="Casablanca (film)">Casablanca</a></i> premières at the Hollywood Theater in New York City.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_27" title="November 27">November 27</a> – WWII: At <a href="/wiki/Toulon" title="Toulon">Toulon</a>, the French navy <a href="/wiki/Scuttling_of_the_French_fleet_in_Toulon" title="Scuttling of the French fleet in Toulon">scuttles its ships and submarines</a> to keep them out of Nazi hands.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_28" title="November 28">November 28</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cocoanut_Grove_fire" title="Cocoanut Grove fire">Cocoanut Grove fire</a>: A fire in the Cocoanut Grove night club in <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a>, kills 491.</li>
<li>The large-scale German "pacification" of the Zamojszczyzna region of Poland begins.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_29" title="November 29">November 29</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Blue_Star_Line" title="Blue Star Line">Blue Star Line</a> <a href="/wiki/Cargo_liner" title="Cargo liner">cargo liner</a> <a href="/wiki/MV_Dunedin_Star" title="MV Dunedin Star">MV&#160;<i>Dunedin Star</i></a> runs aground on the <a href="/wiki/Skeleton_Coast" title="Skeleton Coast">Skeleton Coast</a> of <a href="/wiki/Namibia" title="Namibia">Namibia</a>. Crew and passengers survive following a 26-day overland trek to <a href="/wiki/Windhoek" title="Windhoek">Windhoek</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_30" title="November 30">November 30</a> – WWII: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Tassafaronga" title="Battle of Tassafaronga">Battle of Tassafaronga</a> – In a nighttime naval battle as part of the <a href="/wiki/Guadalcanal_Campaign" title="Guadalcanal Campaign">Guadalcanal Campaign</a>, ships of the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Imperial Japanese Navy</a> defeat those of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_1" title="December 1">December 1</a> – <a href="/wiki/Gasoline" title="Gasoline">Gasoline</a> rationing begins in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_2" title="December 2">December 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/Manhattan_Project" title="Manhattan Project">Manhattan Project</a>: Below the bleachers of Stagg Field at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Chicago" title="University of Chicago">University of Chicago</a>, a team led by <a href="/wiki/Enrico_Fermi" title="Enrico Fermi">Enrico Fermi</a> initiates the first self-sustaining <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_chain_reaction" title="Nuclear chain reaction">nuclear chain reaction</a> (a coded message, "The Italian navigator has landed in the new world" is then sent to U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_4" title="December 4">December 4</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a>: In <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a>, two women, <a href="/wiki/Zofia_Kossak" class="mw-redirect" title="Zofia Kossak">Zofia Kossak and Wanda Filipowicz</a>, risk their lives by setting up the Council for the Assistance of the Jews.</li>
<li>WWII: USAAF bombers make their first raid on Italy.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_7" title="December 7">December 7</a> – WWII: British commandos conduct <a href="/wiki/Operation_Frankton" title="Operation Frankton">Operation Frankton</a>, a raid on shipping in <a href="/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> harbour.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a> – A fire at <a href="/wiki/Seacliff_Lunatic_Asylum" title="Seacliff Lunatic Asylum">Seacliff Lunatic Asylum</a> in New Zealand kills 39 patients.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_17" title="December 17">December 17</a> – The Allies issue the <a href="/wiki/Joint_Declaration_by_Members_of_the_United_Nations" title="Joint Declaration by Members of the United Nations">Joint Declaration by Members of the United Nations</a>, the first time they publicly acknowledge the <a href="/wiki/Holocaust" class="mw-redirect" title="Holocaust">Holocaust</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_22" title="December 22">December 22</a>
<ul>
<li>An avalanche in <a href="/wiki/Aliquippa,_Pennsylvania" title="Aliquippa, Pennsylvania">Aliquippa, Pennsylvania</a>, kills 26, including Vulcan Crucible Steel heir-apparent Samuel A. Stafford Sr., when two 100 ton boulders fall on a bus filled with wartime steel workers on their way home.</li>
<li>An airplane carrying prominent Ustashe general <a href="/wiki/Jure_Franceti%C4%87" title="Jure Francetić">Jure Francetić</a> crashes. Francetić dies as result of the injuries on <a href="/wiki/December_27" title="December 27">December 27</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">December 24</a> – French <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Darlan" title="François Darlan">Admiral Darlan</a>, the former <a href="/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy</a> leader who has switched over to the Allies following the Torch landings, is assassinated in <a href="/wiki/Algiers" title="Algiers">Algiers</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_27" title="December 27">December 27</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Union_of_Pioneers_of_Yugoslavia" title="Union of Pioneers of Yugoslavia">Union of Pioneers of Yugoslavia</a> is founded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_28" title="December 28">December 28</a> – North Atlantic <a href="/wiki/Convoy_ON_154" title="Convoy ON 154">Convoy ON 154</a> is heavily attacked by <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> sinking thirteen ships.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/DDT" class="mw-redirect" title="DDT">DDT</a> is first used as a <a href="/wiki/Pesticide" title="Pesticide">pesticide</a>.</li>
<li>1942 <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> competition in <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">Association football</a>, which <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a> sought to host, is not held, due to World War II.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Births">Births</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1942&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Births">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li>Dame <a href="/wiki/Marcela_Contreras" title="Marcela Contreras">Marcela Contreras</a>, Chilean-British immunologist and educator</li>

</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/January_14" title="January 14">January 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Yogesh_Kumar_Sabharwal" title="Yogesh Kumar Sabharwal">Yogesh Kumar Sabharwal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Justice_of_India" title="Chief Justice of India">Chief Justice of India</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_16" title="January 16">January 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9_Ang%C3%A9lil" title="René Angélil">René Angélil</a>, Canadian singer and manager (d. <a href="/wiki/2016" title="2016">2016</a>)</li>

</ul>
</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/January_27" title="January 27">January 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/John_Witherspoon_(actor)" title="John Witherspoon (actor)">John Witherspoon (actor)</a>, American actor and comedian</li>

<div class="thumb tright">

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_3" title="December 3">December 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Wilhelm_Junk" title="Wilhelm Junk">Wilhelm Junk</a>, Czechoslovakian natural historian, bibliographer and entomologist (b. <a href="/wiki/1866" title="1866">1866</a>)</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/December_6" title="December 6">December 6</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Karl_Herxheimer" title="Karl Herxheimer">Karl Herxheimer</a>, German dermatologist (b. <a href="/wiki/1861" title="1861">1861</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amos_Rusie" title="Amos Rusie">Amos Rusie</a>, American baseball player and <a href="/wiki/MLB_Hall_of_Fame" class="mw-redirect" title="MLB Hall of Fame">MLB Hall of Famer</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1871" title="1871">1871</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_7" title="December 7">December 7</a> – <a href="/wiki/Orland_Steen_Loomis" title="Orland Steen Loomis">Orland Steen Loomis</a>, Governor of Wisconsin (b. <a href="/wiki/1893" title="1893">1893</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a>
<ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Albert_Kahn_(architect)" title="Albert Kahn (architect)">Albert Kahn</a>, American architect (b. <a href="/wiki/1869" title="1869">1869</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_9" title="December 9">December 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9raphine_Louis" title="Séraphine Louis">Séraphine Louis</a>, French painter (b. <a href="/wiki/1864" title="1864">1864</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_12" title="December 12">December 12</a>
<ul>

</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_13" title="December 13">December 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hakeem_Fateh_Mohammad_Sehwani" title="Hakeem Fateh Mohammad Sehwani">Hakeem Fateh Mohammad Sehwani</a>, Indian scholar, poet, literary, journalist and politician (b. <a href="/wiki/1882" title="1882">1882</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wlodimir_Led%C3%B3chowski" title="Wlodimir Ledóchowski">Wlodimir Ledóchowski</a>, Polish <a href="/wiki/Jesuit" class="mw-redirect" title="Jesuit">Jesuit</a> priest and servant of God (b. <a href="/wiki/1866" title="1866">1866</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Carl_Gustav_Fleischer" title="Carl Gustav Fleischer">Carl Gustav Fleischer</a>, Norwegian general (b. <a href="/wiki/1883" title="1883">1883</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_21" title="December 21">December 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Franz_Boas" title="Franz Boas">Franz Boas</a>, German anthropologist (b. <a href="/wiki/1858" title="1858">1858</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_22" title="December 22">December 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Robert_Kosch" title="Robert Kosch">Robert Kosch</a>, Prussian general (b. <a href="/wiki/1856" title="1856">1856</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_23" title="December 23">December 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Konstantin_Balmont" title="Konstantin Balmont">Konstantin Balmont</a>, Soviet poet and translator (b. <a href="/wiki/1867" title="1867">1867</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">December 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Darlan" title="François Darlan">François Darlan</a>, French admiral and politician, 81st <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister of France</a> (assassinated) (b. <a href="/wiki/1881" title="1881">1881</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_27" title="December 27">December 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/William_G._Morgan" title="William G. Morgan">William G. Morgan</a>, inventor of volleyball (b. <a href="/wiki/1870" title="1870">1870</a>)</li>

</ul>
